Plugger

Pretty straight forward. Someone post three words, and you carry on.

Like this:
A: Harry Potter was
B: Hugging Lord Voldemort
C: When Ron Measly
B: And Hermione Stranger
C: Discovered the Chamber
A: Of Cheese. Then...

And so on. I'll start:
